< text>
I love this place!  I only take my dogs for nail trims since I bathe/groom them myself.  So, I can't write about any other service, but as far as nail trimming goes, they are the cheapest around.  Sara always does my really difficult dog and is always so friendly -- helps me leash up the 4 girls when I'm done and even helps me put them in the car.  The other groomers are also very friendly and helpful.  I've read some poor reviews about the Paw House where people have said they would never take their dogs there again for whatever reason.  Like doing business with any other vendor/business, if you have concerns prior to having a service done, take the time to talk with the service people so that hopefully you won't have any problems.  Stuff happens in life.  If you have a living being that is being serviced, be proactive to see that the best care is given to your animal.  Be forgiving.  The Paw House would never deliberately hurt your animal  --  they care.</text>

< text>
The manicure/pedicure area is more luxurious than womens salons. We have our own TV with Direct TV remote and headphones. The chairs are wide Super kush leather seats. They really push to sell you a membership. Unless you plan to use thier services a least twice a month I don't see the value in it. A smaller membership package I would be interested in. Also a haircut priced for someone that does not have enough hair to style would be nice as well.</text>

< review>
I cannot speak highly enough about Joey who works at this location!  I strolled in looking for a u bar for a women’s bike so I could mount it properly on my bike rack.  It pretty much goes from the seat to the fork so you can hang a women’s bike on a bike rack.  They had exactly what I needed.  As I was paying Joey asked me a couple questions regarding the women’s bike I clearly just bought as the tags were still on it from the big red box store across the street, that was upside down, yes upside down as it was the only way I could get it on the rack to go find a u bar lol.  He gave me a very friendly warning that the bike was most likely put together like sh*t and to be very careful before I gave it to my fiancé to ride.  He explained everything I should I check and tighten from the brakes all the way down to greasing axels.  He was extremely polite and not once did he try and sell me a tune up from his own store.  He just explained in depth why it was important and what to do.  I couldn’t have thanked him enough.  Following that conversation he came outside with me to make sure the u bar was a good fit, within a minute the seat popped off like he warned me in the store, so I was dead in the water with trying to use the u bar, he then pointed out why the bike felt so out of sorts from the seat to the fact the handlebars were angled completely wrong along with the brake levers  and gear shifters.  He said “I can’t let you leave like this, hang on.”  He went inside and came back out with and handful of wrenches, re installed and fixed the seat height and angle, tightened up anything he could in the parking lot and pointed out about 5-7 things that were exactly what he was referring to in the store from loose bolts to ones that were installed a*s backwards.  After that he helped me mount the bike and make sure it was secure.  By the time he was done I actually felt guilty for not buying a bike from him personally.  Again I cannot thank you enough Joey and for anyone reading this review you would be out of your mind to go to a different shop.  I have been to plenty where unless your dropping $2k on a bike you don’t matter, never mind a $40 u bar for a bike you bought at a box store.  I HIGHLY HIGHLY recommend Napa Valley Velo, and I will 100% be back to buy a bike for myself.  Joey you are the definition of good customer service!!!  I listened to everything you said and after about 90 minutes in my garage turning my own wrenches I think the bike is ready to go!  Again THANK YOU!!!<//review>

<userid>114316374457266226890< /userid><Name>Brandon Reilly<//Name><date>1529292248456</date><rating>5<//rating><text>Great, small but high energy venue for concerts located right near the Disney Theme Parks and Honda Stadium area of Anaheim, CA.  The design style is classic Howard Hughes style metropolitan Art Deco (think Batman 1989 and the animated series or the Rocketeer). The actual stage "seating" area is four "tiers" each separated by a wall. No installed chairs or anything. Rock and metal concerts benefit greatly from this since it becomes easily foot-navigated standing room only. Other more specialized concerts will see them putting out rows of chairs. There is ample parking in their paid lot which reaches all the way to the venue's front gate area ($12 at the time of this review, June 2018).<//text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP-BTA09JhmKQdef4S3hMJPSKz2kZdQ4y9tbpH4=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pictures><resp>None</resp>< gmapID>

<Date>1547743282851<//Date>< Review>
Immaculately clean and upscale modern music venue. A lot different than the seedy dive bars I frequent to check out live music, but I won't let any of that cleanliness rub off on me.
I saw Henry Rollins' traveling slide show here, and this was a good place for that. Tiered flooring in the house gives good sightlines to the performer throughout.
My main complaint was how early they shut the bar down. This makes me sad. Also not sure what's up with the Uber pick up spot. Was stopping in the driveway and blocking egress traffic really the plan?</Review>

<text>I came here recently to see Kevin James stand-up comedy. He was hilarious!

This isn't a bad theater. Anywhere is pretty much a good seat, unless you have the unfortunate luck to sit behind a very tall person, which has happened to me once or twice. Since each row isn't elevated as you work your way to the back of the theater, you could end up having an obstructed view of the stage by the person(s) in front of you.

Parking is pretty easy to find. I usually arrive 30 minutes before any show and have no trouble finding a spot right up front. When you leave a show, prepare to wait at least 20-30 mins to get out, unless you park right by the exit. There's only a couple of exit lanes, so it takes a bit longer to leave.< /text>< gmapID>

< text>
Nice Concert/music/event venue - Conveniently Located

This venue is right between the 5 fwy and the 57 freeway, doesn't matter if you're coming from LA, of the the IE Empire is conveniently located.

- The venue had a makeover a few years ago,  and there have been some remodeling inside/outside as well, there is plenty of parking lot, last time I was there they charged me $12, not sure is the parking rate changes depending on the event.

- Inside they have drinks, soft drinks, and pretty big for a venue, not sure how many people it fits.<//text>

<Review>We saw Todrick Hall at the Grove in July '16. The Grove has a large parking area and well trained parking attendants who kept the line moving and got everyone parked much faster than I had expected. The seating area itself was smaller than I had imagined when purchasing tickets, which worked to our favor; when we asked a seating attendant to point us in the right direction, we were happily surprised to see him heading right up towards the stage. We had seating so close I could easily see the performers face. The Grove also has conveniently placed large, flat screen TVs that feed out the performance for those that want a super close look. The seating was comfortable enough, we were hip to hip, although once the show started nobody cared :p< /Review><name>Elisabeth Breeze< /name><GmapID>0x80dcd7996d053379:0xfaba57ce9ef0682<//GmapID><userid>103495612245260822316</userid>< Rate>

<Text>I'm not a fan of standing room only events, however the City National Grove has the best possible standing room only layout in my mind.  By breaking the venue into multiple rows of standing room only you don't have the surge of people crushing you against a wall and the crowds  generally seem good natured. <rate>4< /rate><review>PARKING:
Plenty of one level parking although we ubered, I think I read it was $15

SERVICE/STAFF:
service staff were super friendly and tried really hard even though the dinner service before the show was chaotic & disorganized(we were in tier two dinner table seating). The dinner option is good. Their is a full bar and your server comes to your table and takes your drink and food orders. There is a decent small menu of 1 salad, 4 entree options, & 1 desert which I recommend. Ours was one leafy green salad to start, then there were surf&turf, a chicken marsala, and vegetarian raviole entree to choose from & a vanilla cream brulee for desert. The shrimp and twice baked potato from the surf & turf was especially good. If you dont do the dinner option, there are also snack bars in different areas where you can buy sandwiches & other snacks to eat in the show.

THEATRE:
The theatre itself is a newer modern auditorium with good acoustics. Bathrooms are clean & convenient<//review>< Pics>
None<//Pics>
